Amen"; not the hedging of a man unsure of his ground — Moroni puts his own authority on the table and tells the reader you'll find out whether I had it when you MEET ME, for we'll stand before God together at the judgment; a claim only makeable by someone certain he'll be there, the reader will be there, and the meeting will vindicate him; for Joseph Smith literal — he DID see Moroni face to face; for the rest of us future, but Moroni writes as one who will personally meet every reader at the bar of God and answer for what he wrote — a bracing accountability, not an anonymous ancient voice but a man who'll look his readers in the eye at the judgment]→ 5:6 (Moro 10:27; 2 Ne 33:11; Jacob 6:13; Moro 10:34)

### from Ether 6
- `doctrine:the-storm-that-buries-them-is-the-wind-that-drives-them-home` —[God does not give calm seas but "a furious wind"; they are "many times buried in the depths of the sea, because of the mountain waves... and the great and terrible tempests" — BURIED, submerged again and again; yet the same wind that buries does the one thing they need: "the wind did never cease to blow TOWARDS THE PROMISED LAND while they were upon the waters"; one of the most important pictures of affliction in scripture — the storm that nearly drowns them is the very thing driving them home; God didn't calm the wind, He AIMED it; the affliction itself was not an obstacle to the journey but the means of it; sometimes the storm is not the enemy of your journey but its engine, the same wind that buries you blowing you home]→ 6:5-8 (Ether 2:24-25; 1 Ne 18:8-13; Ps 107:23-30; Rom 8:28)
- `doctrine:praise-all-the-day-long-in-the-storm-gratitude-in-the-tempest` —["he did thank and praise the Lord all the day long; and when the night came, they did not cease to praise the Lord"; buried in the deep, tossed by mountain waves, in a sealed barge for the better part of a year — and the response is PRAISE, not complaint, not the murmuring Laman and Lemuel offered in their storm (1 Ne 18:9); the same man chastened three chapters ago for NEGLECTING prayer for four years (2:14) now will not stop praising; the transformation complete; he can praise in the storm because he understands what it's doing — carrying them home; gratitude in the tempest is faith that it's in God's hand and aimed at the promise]→ 6:9-10 (1 Ne 18:9-16; Ps 34:1-3; Mosiah 26:39; Ether 2:14)
- `doctrine:the-light-God-gives-holds-even-under-the-waves` —["they did have light continually, whether it was above the water or under the water"; the stones God touched shone even in the depths — the light He gave did not fail when they were submerged; the light held under the waves; so does His presence — the faith-light that carries through the storm doesn't go out when you're buried in it]→ 6:10 (Ether 3:4-6; D&C 88:11-13; John 1:5; Ps 139:11-12)
- `theme:the-journey-through-the-storm-ends-in-worship-and-tears-of-joy` —["when they had set their feet upon the shores of the promised land they bowed themselves down upon the face of the land, and did humble themselves before the Lord, and did shed tears of joy before the Lord, because of the multitude of his tender mercies over them"; 344 days on the water (echoing Noah's flood) and the first act on solid ground is WORSHIP — bowing, humbling, weeping for joy at God's "tender mercies" (the phrase Nephi opened with, 1 Ne 1:20); the journey through the storm ends not in relief or self-congratulation but in tears of gratitude; the people who praised through the tempest now weep with thanksgiving on the shore]→ 6:11-12 (1 Ne 1:20; Ps 116:12-14; Gen 8:13-20; Alma 26:8)
- `doctrine:surely-this-thing-leadeth-into-captivity-the-anti-monarchy-warning` —[the people ask to anoint a king, and the brother of Jared's response is immediate and grieved: "this was grievous unto them... Surely this thing leadeth into captivity"; the same anti-monarchy wisdom Samuel gave Israel (1 Sam 8:10-18) and Mosiah built his reform on (Mosiah 29) — a king concentrates power in one fallible man, the people's liberty hostage to his righteousness; the brother of Jared sees at the very founding where it leads, and the ENTIRE book of Ether is the proof — the Jaredite kings dethroning/imprisoning/murdering one another across generations, the people repeatedly in captivity; he saw it on day one, but Jared overruled him]→ 6:22-24 (1 Sam 8:10-18; Mosiah 23:7-13; Mosiah 29:16-23; Ether 7:5)
- `doctrine:kingship-cannot-be-forced-constrain-no-man-to-be-your-king` —[Pagag, the firstborn chosen king, "refused and would not be their king"; the people would that his father constrain him, "but his father would not; and he commanded them that they should constrain no man to be their king"; even the king must CONSENT — the office cannot be imposed; one bright detail in the founding of a monarchy that will lead to captivity — at least the throne is not forced on an unwilling man]→ 6:25-27 (Mosiah 29:38-39; D&C 121:39; 2 Cor 9:7; Philem 1:14)
- `theme:a-good-first-king-delays-but-does-not-remove-the-structural-danger` —[Orihah, the first king, is righteous — he "did walk humbly before the Lord, and did remember how great things the Lord had done for his father, and also taught his people"; the institution begins well, with a good man who remembers and teaches; but the warning "this thing leadeth into captivity" stands over the whole book like a shadow — a good first king does not undo the structural danger of concentrated power, it only delays it; the Jaredites will spend the rest of Ether proving the brother of Jared right]→ 6:28-30 (Mosiah 29:25-32; Hel 5:2; 1 Sam 8:9; Eccl 8:9)

### from Ether 7
- `doctrine:the-captivity-cycle-begins-the-brother-of-Jareds-warning-vindicated` —[Corihor rebels against his father Kib and "took him captive, which brought to pass the saying of the brother of Jared that they would be brought into captivity"; the warning of 6:23 fulfilled in the very next generation but one — a king anointed, within two generations a son raising an army against his father and imprisoning him; the structural danger the brother of Jared saw — concentrate the nation's power in one throne, and the throne becomes the prize men will kill for; the captivity is the monarchy's natural fruit; the rest of Ether is this same cycle turning over and over, exactly as foretold]→ 7:4-5 (Ether 6:23; Ether 8:3-4; Ether 10:14; 1 Sam 8:11-18)
- `doctrine:God-preserves-the-lineage-even-in-captivity-the-deliverer-born-in-the-dungeon` —["Kib dwelt in captivity... nevertheless Kib begat Shule in his old age, while he was yet in captivity"; the king imprisoned, the kingdom usurped — and yet in prison the line continues, and the son born in captivity (Shule) is the one who'll restore the kingdom; God's purposes not defeated by the captivity, the deliverer born inside the very imprisonment; the pattern throughout scripture (Moses born under Pharaoh's death-decree, Joseph rising through the Egyptian prison) — the deliverance grows up inside the bondage; the line is not cut, the deliverer may already be growing up in the dark]→ 7:7 (Ex 1:22-2:10; Gen 39-41; Acts 7:9-10; Isa 9:2)
- `doctrine:restoration-not-vengeance-power-given-to-the-repentant-enemy` —[Shule defeats Corihor and could exact retribution, but instead "restored [the kingdom] unto his father Kib" — fought not to seize power for himself but to give it back to the rightful king; and when Corihor, the brother who imprisoned their father, REPENTS, "Shule gave him power in his kingdom"; the man with every right to destroy his treacherous brother instead gave him power upon repentance; the rare interruption of the vengeance-cycle — a victor who restores rather than usurps, answering a repentant enemy with trust not retribution; the opposite of the vengeance-oath that destroyed the Nephites (Morm 3); the cycle CAN be broken for a generation by a man who refuses vengeance]→ 7:9, 13 (Gen 45:4-8; Mosiah 3:11-12; Matt 5:44; Morm 3:9-15)
- `doctrine:the-righteous-king-protects-the-prophets-freedom-to-preach` —[prophets come "prophesying that the wickedness and idolatry of the people was bringing a curse upon the land," the people "revile against the prophets, and did mock them"; the fork that decides a nation's fate, and Shule chooses rightly — rather than joining the mockery or silencing the prophets (as Noah did to Abinadi, as the latter Jaredite kings will), "king Shule did execute judgment against all those who did revile against the prophets" and "did execute a law... which gave power unto the prophets that they should go whithersoever they would"; the righteous king uses the throne's power to PROTECT the prophetic voice; the result that saves a people: "by this cause the people were brought unto repentance"; political power ought to protect the prophetic word not control or silence it, because the nation's survival depends on the people being able to HEAR the call to repent]→ 7:23-25 (Mosiah 29:25-32; Alma 30:7-11; D&C 134:1-9; Mosiah 17:7-20)
- `theme:the-righteous-king-remembers-what-God-did-for-the-fathers` —[Shule "remembered the great things that the Lord had done for his fathers in bringing them across the great deep; wherefore he did execute judgment in righteousness all his days"; the same remembering that marked Orihah (6:30) — the righteous king is the one who remembers what God did for the fathers, and that memory keeps him in righteousness; the protected prophet → the repentant people → the spared nation, and the remembering king sustains it all]→ 7:26-27 (Ether 6:30; Deut 8:18; Hel 12:2; Mosiah 2:41)

### from Ether 8
- `doctrine:the-wicked-mine-the-record-for-the-methods-of-evil` —["Hath he not read the record which our fathers brought across the great deep?... is there not an account concerning them of old, that they by their secret plans did obtain kingdoms and great glory?"; the daughter of Jared found the secret combinations IN THE RECORD — a sobering counterpoint to the record-as-sacred-witness theme; the same kind of record that preserves the words of Christ can preserve the methods of evil, and the wicked will mine it; knowledge preserved is morally neutral until a heart takes it up — the righteous find Christ, the ambitious find "secret plans"; the record is a mirror]→ 8:9 (Hel 6:26-30; 3 Ne 6:28; Moses 5:30; Gen 3:13)
- `doctrine:secret-combinations-trace-to-Cain-and-are-kept-up-by-the-power-of-the-devil` —["the oaths which were given by them of old who also sought power, which had been handed down EVEN FROM CAIN, who was a murderer from the beginning... they were kept up by the power of the devil... to keep them in darkness, to help such as sought power to gain power, and to murder, and to plunder, and to lie"; the deep root the BoM traces under every secret combination (Gadianton, the Jaredite conspiracies) — back to Cain's covenant with Satan (Moses 5:29-31); always the same pattern — an oath of secrecy, mutual protection enforced by death, power and gain through murder; not a human political tool but satanic INFRASTRUCTURE; "most abominable and wicked above all in the sight of God" — His strongest condemnation reserved for the organized, sworn, secret pursuit of power through bloodshed]→ 8:15-18 (Hel 6:26-30; Moses 5:29-31; Gen 4:7-8; 2 Ne 9:9)
- `doctrine:the-Lord-worketh-not-in-secret-the-secrecy-itself-is-the-tell` —["the Lord worketh not in secret combinations, neither doth he will that man should shed blood, but in all things hath forbidden it, from the beginning of man"; the clean contrast exposing the secret combination as a COUNTERFEIT of God's work — God works in the open, His word "upon the house-tops" (Morm 5:8); the secret combination inverts every term (secret vs open, murder vs the forbidding of blood, power-over vs freeing); the secrecy itself is the tell — anything that requires an oath of concealment, cannot bear the light, binds men by fear of death not to divulge it, is by that very fact opposed to God; a usable discernment: the work of God can always stand in the open, the work of the devil requires the dark]→ 8:19 (Morm 5:8; D&C 38:13; 2 Ne 26:22-23; John 3:20-21)
- `doctrine:Moroni-breaks-the-chain-by-refusing-to-write-the-oaths` —["I, Moroni, do not write the manner of their oaths and combinations, for it hath been made known unto me that they are had among all people"; where the daughter of Jared REVIVED the dark knowledge by reading it out of the record, Moroni BREAKS THE CHAIN by refusing to record it; he'll warn that secret combinations exist and are deadly but won't transmit the METHOD; some knowledge is dangerous precisely in its preservation, and the faithful record-keeper exercises restraint about what he passes on; the inverse of the daughter of Jared; the record-keeper's discipline includes WITHHOLDING — to write certain things is to arm the wicked]→ 8:20 (Morm 8:35; 3 Ne 26:18; Ether 13:18; Prov 11:13)
- `doctrine:secret-combinations-destroyed-both-civilizations-and-seek-to-overthrow-the-freedom-of-all-lands` —["they have caused the destruction of this people [the Jaredites]... and also the destruction of the people of Nephi... whoso buildeth it up seeketh to overthrow the freedom of all lands, nations, and countries; and it bringeth to pass the destruction of all people, for it is built up by the devil, who is the father of all lies"; BOTH civilizations on this land destroyed by the same disease; the secret combination's ultimate aim is not local power but the overthrow of FREEDOM ITSELF — of all lands, nations, and countries; the devil's instrument for the destruction of human liberty everywhere, because the devil who beguiled our first parents has always sought to control rather than free]→ 8:21-25 (Hel 6:28; Morm 8:21; Moses 4:1-4; 2 Ne 2:27)
- `doctrine:awake-to-a-sense-of-your-awful-situation` —["the Lord commandeth you, when ye shall see these things come among you that ye shall awake to a sense of your awful situation, because of this secret combination which shall be among you"; Moroni speaks as one shown our day (Morm 8:35); the summons OUT OF COMPLACENCY — secret combinations work by remaining unseen, and the first defense is simply to RECOGNIZE them, to wake up to the fact that organized, hidden pursuit of power and gain is operating; "suffer not that these murderous combinations shall get above you"]→ 8:23-24 (3 Ne 16:10; Morm 8:35; 2 Ne 28:32; D&C 42:64)
- `theme:the-warning-is-written-that-evil-may-be-done-away-not-to-frighten-but-to-free` —["I, Moroni, am commanded to write these things THAT EVIL MAY BE DONE AWAY, and that the time may come that Satan may have no power upon the hearts of the children of men, but that they may be persuaded to do good continually, that they may come unto the fountain of all righteousness and be saved"; the purpose of exposing the secret combination is its undoing — that evil be done away, Satan lose his grip, men be turned toward good; Moroni warns not to frighten but to free; the same Moroni who refuses to write the oaths writes the warning, so the reader awake to the danger can resist it and come to Christ; the exposure of the darkness in service of the light]→ 8:26 (2 Ne 30:18; Moro 7:12-13; Mosiah 5:2; John 8:32)

### from Ether 9
- `doctrine:the-secret-combination-devours-its-own-evil-organized-for-power-is-suicidal` —[Akish's combination seizes the kingdom then turns on itself — Akish murders the king (Jared) who made the deal with him, starves his own son to death, his sons buy the people's loyalty and war on their father; the war "lasted... unto the destruction of nearly all the people of the kingdom, yea, even all, save it were thirty souls"; a conspiracy built to seize power ended by destroying nearly everyone including the conspirators; the self-consuming nature of evil (Morm 4:5) — the secret combination doesn't deliver the power it promises, it devours those who serve it, because the same oath-bound treachery that gains the throne is available to whoever wants it next]→ 9:1-12 (Morm 4:5; Ether 8:21-22; Hel 6:28; Gal 6:7-8)
- `doctrine:deliverance-by-obedient-withdrawal-the-faithful-flee-the-warning-and-outlast-the-wicked` —["the Lord warned Omer in a dream that he should depart out of the land; wherefore Omer departed"; the one man preserved is the one who heeded the warning and fled, and was "restored again to the land of his inheritance" when the conspirators had destroyed themselves; the faithful man who removes himself from the path of the combination survives it — he didn't fight it, he obeyed God's word to depart and outlasted it; sometimes deliverance from organized evil is not confrontation but obedient withdrawal — getting out of the way at God's word and letting the wicked consume each other]→ 9:3, 13 (Gen 19:15-17; 1 Ne 2:1-3; Matt 2:13; D&C 5:24)
- `doctrine:the-choice-land-decree-restated-at-the-height-of-prosperity` —[at the very height of prosperity — "exceedingly rich" with fruit, grain, silks, fine linen, gold, silver, herds — the Lord restates the decree: "whoso should possess the land should possess it unto the Lord, or they should be destroyed when they were ripened in iniquity"; the reminder comes precisely when prosperity might tempt them to forget — the decree of Ether 2 spoken again at the moment of plenty, because plenty is exactly when a people stops thinking it could ever be swept off]→ 9:20 (Ether 2:8-12; 1 Ne 2:20; 2 Ne 1:5-9; Deut 8:11-18)
- `doctrine:another-righteous-Jaredite-saw-the-Son-of-Righteousness` —["he even saw the Son of Righteousness, and did rejoice and glory in his day; and he died in peace"; like the brother of Jared, the righteous king Emer SAW the premortal Christ — "the Son of Righteousness," the Malachi 4:2 title (3 Ne 25:2); the brother of Jared's vision was unprecedented in its FULLNESS but not the only Jaredite sighting of Christ; the God of the Jaredites was Christ, and the righteous among them beheld Him; datapoint adjacent to is-jesus-christ-god]→ 9:22 (Ether 3:14; 3 Ne 25:2; Mal 4:2; Ether 9:22)
- `doctrine:the-wicked-king-silences-the-prophets-casting-them-into-pits` —[Heth "embrace[s] the secret plans again of old, to destroy his father," murders Com with his own sword, and when prophets come crying repentance "the people believed not... but they cast them out; and some of them they cast into pits and left them to perish... according to the commandment of the king, Heth"; the wicked king silences the prophets — the exact inverse of Shule who PROTECTED them (7:23-25) and saw his people repent; the word the people reject comes true upon them — the famine and serpents the prophets warned of arrive]→ 9:26-31 (Ether 7:23-25; Mosiah 17:7-20; Jer 38:6; 1 Kgs 22:27)
- `doctrine:the-affliction-does-what-the-prophets-word-could-not-but-the-moment-they-humble-themselves-He-spares-them` —["when the people saw that they must perish they began to repent of their iniquities and cry unto the Lord... when they had humbled themselves sufficiently before the Lord he did send rain"; the affliction (famine + serpents) does what the prophets' words could not — they would not repent at the preaching, they repented at the brink of extinction; the recurring tragedy and mercy — God prefers to reach a people through the prophet's word, but when they silence the prophet He reaches them through affliction; even then, the moment they humble themselves He spares them; the famine was not the end of His mercy but the form His mercy had to take when the gentler form was cast into a pit; the people who would not hear the prophet heard the hunger]→ 9:34-35 (Alma 32:13-16; Hel 12:3; Mosiah 21:14-15; Alma 34:34-35)
- `theme:the-honest-transliteration-cureloms-and-cumoms` —["they also had horses, and asses, and there were elephants and cureloms and cumoms; all of which were useful unto man, and more especially the elephants and cureloms and cumoms"; Joseph Smith transliterated two unknown Jaredite animal-names rather than guessing at an English equivalent; an honesty in that — the translator left untranslated what he did not know rather than inventing a familiar word; a small instance of the record's own integrity, better to preserve the unknown term than fabricate certainty]→ 9:19 (Mosiah 8:11; Ether 9:17; 1 Ne 18:25)

### from Ether 10
- `doctrine:the-kings-righteousness-is-the-hinge-of-the-peoples-blessing` —[Moroni's roll of kings is an argument, not mere genealogy — "when righteousness prevails, the people are blessed and prospered by the Lord"; a controlled demonstration of the choice-land decree at the level of the individual reign — Shez remembers and builds "a righteous kingdom" (prosperity), Riplakish forgets and oppresses (the people crushed, then rebel), Levi/Corom/Kish/Lib do right and the land flourishes; the king's righteousness is the hinge on which the people's blessing turns; a nation under a throne rises and falls with the soul of the man on it — the danger the brother of Jared named, the people's welfare hostage to one fallible man's character]→ 10:1-2, 28 (Ether 6:23; Ether 2:8-12; 1 Ne 2:20; Prov 29:2)
- `doctrine:the-anatomy-of-tyranny-monuments-built-on-the-backs-of-the-oppressed` —[Riplakish "did lay that upon men's shoulders which was grievous to be borne; yea, he did tax them with heavy taxes; and with the taxes he did build many spacious buildings... an exceedingly beautiful throne... many prisons, and whoso would not be subject unto taxes he did cast into prison... whoso refused to labor he did cause to be put to death. Wherefore he did obtain all his fine work, yea, even his fine gold he did cause to be refined in prison"; the BoM's sharpest study of tyranny — monumental wealth and beauty extracted from the forced labor of the poor, the throne and spacious buildings literally built on the backs of imprisoned men; the great-and-spacious building (1 Ne 8:26) made into a regime — pride that builds its monuments on the suffering of those it crushes]→ 10:5-7 (1 Ne 8:26-27; Mosiah 11:3-15; 1 Kgs 12:4; Ex 1:11-14)
- `doctrine:oppression-manufactures-the-rebellion-that-ends-it` —[after forty-two years "the people did rise up in rebellion against him; and... Riplakish was killed, and his descendants were driven out of the land"; the moral realism the record doesn't flinch from — a tyrant who grinds his people for his own glory will in the end be thrown down by the very people he ground; oppression is not stable, it manufactures the rebellion that ends it]→ 10:8 (Prov 28:15-16; Mosiah 29:21-23; Ex 1:11-14; Mosiah 11:20-29)
- `doctrine:public-justice-without-personal-righteousness-does-not-save` —[Morianton "did do justice unto the people, but not unto himself because of his many whoredoms; wherefore he was cut off from the presence of the Lord"; a ruler who governed WELL — eased the people's burden, did them justice, beloved enough that "they did anoint him king" — yet "cut off from the presence of the Lord" by private sin; public justice and personal righteousness are not the same, and the first doesn't save a man who lacks the second; a person can be genuinely just to others and still destroy his soul by the sins he keeps private; the good he did for others was real but couldn't stand in for the righteousness he refused himself]→ 10:11 (Matt 23:25-28; Alma 39:3-5; D&C 121:37; 1 Cor 9:27)
- `doctrine:the-most-prospered-people-are-not-the-happiest-material-peak-vs-the-love-of-God` —["never could be a people more blessed than were they, and more prospered by the hand of the Lord... in a land that was choice above all lands"; set beside 4 Ne 1:16's "could not be a happier people" — the difference is everything: the Nephite Zion was the HAPPIEST because "the love of God did dwell in the hearts of the people" (no contention, all things common, no -ites); the Jaredite peak under Lib is the MOST PROSPERED — industry, ore, silks, fine workmanship, material abundance; one a peak of the heart, the other a peak of the economy; the Jaredites at their height had everything the world calls blessing and it did not save them, because material prosperity is not the love of God; the most-prospered people are not necessarily the happiest, and prosperity by itself sets up the pride that destroys]→ 10:19-28 (4 Ne 1:15-16; Hel 6:9-11; Hel 12:2; Deut 8:11-18)
- `doctrine:when-the-secret-combination-is-entrenched-beyond-a-kings-power-the-doom-is-sealed` —["in the days of Com there began to be robbers in the land; and they adopted the old plans, and administered oaths after the manner of the ancients, and sought again to destroy the kingdom. Now Com did fight against them much; NEVERTHELESS, HE DID NOT PREVAIL AGAINST THEM"; the secret combinations back, and for the first time a RIGHTEOUS king "did not prevail against them"; the disease earlier kings could fight off now entrenched beyond a king's power to root out — the turning point of the whole Jaredite decline; when the combination becomes so woven into society that even a king fighting "much" cannot defeat it, the doom is sealed; once the organized oath-bound pursuit of power through murder is beyond rooting out, only complete destruction will end it; Com's failure to prevail is the quiet announcement that the Jaredites have passed the point of recovery]→ 10:33-34 (Ether 8:15-18; Hel 6:38; Hel 2:13-14; Ether 13:18)

### from Ether 11
- `doctrine:God-never-stops-sending-prophets-but-a-people-can-make-themselves-unable-to-hear` —[the prophets come "again," "again," "again" (7:23, 9:28, 11:1, 12, 20) — God never stops sending the warning, the mercy relentless; but the people's response hardens by degrees — first REJECT (11:2), then SEEK TO DESTROY, then KILL them all (11:5), and finally simply WILL NOT HEAR: "the people hardened their hearts... and the prophets mourned and withdrew from among the people" (11:13); the same withdrawal that befell Mormon (Morm 1:16-17), the famine of the word (Amos 8:11-12); a people can push out the very voice that could save them, until the prophets mourn and leave; the silence that follows is not God's abandonment but the consequence of their own deafness]→ 11:1-13 (Ether 7:23; Morm 1:16-17; Amos 8:11-12; 2 Chr 36:15-16)
- `doctrine:the-warning-escalates-as-the-people-harden-mercy-intensifying-not-diminishing` —[early prophets warn of "the destruction of that great people except they should repent" (11:1); by Ethem's day "the Lord would UTTERLY destroy them from off the face of the earth" (11:12); by Coriantor's day "to their UTTER destruction" (11:20); the threat does not soften as time runs out — it sharpens; mercy INTENSIFYING not diminishing — as the danger grows nearer God makes the warning more total, more unmistakable, trying harder to reach a people hearing less; the escalation of the warning tracks the urgency of the love behind it]→ 11:12, 20 (2 Ne 28:32; Hel 13:38; Ether 2:9-10; Luke 19:41-44)
- `doctrine:the-choice-land-passes-to-another-people-God-brings-after-the-same-manner` —["the Lord God would send or bring forth ANOTHER people to possess the land, by his power, after the manner by which he brought their fathers"; the choice-land covenant means the land does not stand empty when a people is swept off — it passes to the next people God brings, exactly as the Jaredites received it; the prophecy of the handoff — the Jaredites replaced by the Lehites (Nephites/Lamanites), brought "after the manner by which he brought their fathers" (the same ocean crossing, the same covenant); the land is the Lord's, He gives it to whom He will in succession on the same terms, and the people who ripen in iniquity make room for the next]→ 11:21 (Omni 1:21; Ether 13:20-21; Deut 29:28; 1 Ne 17:36-38)
- `doctrine:the-secret-combination-makes-a-people-deaf-to-the-prophets` —["they did reject all the words of the prophets, BECAUSE OF THEIR SECRET SOCIETY AND WICKED ABOMINATIONS"; the rejection of the prophetic voice rooted in the secret combination — entrenched beyond a king's power (10:34), it now drives the people to reject every prophet, because the combination CANNOT SURVIVE THE LIGHT the prophets bring; a society organized around oath-bound secrecy, power, and gain has a structural interest in silencing the voice that exposes it; organized hidden evil and deafness to the prophetic word are not two problems but one — the combination makes the people unable to hear, because hearing would mean its undoing; why the silencing of prophets recurs at every stage of both collapses — the combination defending itself]→ 11:15, 22 (Ether 8:15-26; Ether 10:33-34; Hel 6:38; John 3:20)
- `theme:the-book-comes-full-circle-from-the-founding-faith-to-the-lonely-faith-of-Ether` —["Coriantor begat Ether, and he died, having dwelt in captivity all his days"; the genealogy that opened Ether (1:6-32, listed in reverse) now revealed in forward motion as a chain of imprisoned kings, the once-glorious line ending in bondage; Ether — the last prophet, the record's author — born into a people on the brink (kingdom fragmented, combination entrenched, prophets withdrawn, warning escalated to utter destruction, his father dying in captivity); born at the end of the world into the wreckage of a civilization that rejected every prophet sent to it; the book comes full circle — it began with one man (the brother of Jared) crying unto the Lord and being given a choice land, it ends with one man (Ether) crying repentance over that land as it destroys itself]→ 11:23 (Ether 1:6-32; Ether 12:1-3; Ether 15:33-34; 1 Ne 1:4)

### from Ether 12
- `doctrine:ye-receive-no-witness-until-after-the-trial-of-your-faith` —["faith is things which are hoped for and not seen; wherefore, dispute not because ye see not, for ye receive no witness UNTIL AFTER THE TRIAL of your faith"; the law the entire BoM has demonstrated, stated as a principle — the witness comes AFTER the trial of faith, never before; the sign-seeker has it backwards (see first, then believe), but faith by definition acts before it sees, the seeing the reward of the acting not its precondition; walk into the dark before the light comes, plant the seed before you taste the fruit (Alma 32), make the sixteen stones before God touches them (Ether 3); to wait for the witness before exercising faith is to wait forever]→ 12:6 (Heb 11:1; Alma 32:21-43; 3 Ne 26:11; John 20:29)
- `doctrine:the-roll-of-faith-every-miracle-came-after-faith` —[the BoM's Hebrews 11 — "by faith Christ showed himself unto our fathers... he showed not himself until after their faith"; "if there be no faith among the children of men God can do no miracle among them" (faith the CONDITION of the miracle); examples each echo a chapter walked — Alma and Amulek + the prison walls (Alma 14), Nephi and Lehi + the change on the Lamanites (Hel 5), Ammon (Alma 17-26), the three disciples; "neither at any time hath any wrought miracles until after their faith"; the climax is the brother of Jared who "could not be kept from within the veil" (Moroni's commentary on Ether 3) — faith perfected breaks the veil; every manifestation of God's power came AFTER faith, on the far side of the trial]→ 12:7-21 (Heb 11:1-40; Alma 14:26-29; Hel 5:45-52; Ether 3:6-20)
- `doctrine:I-give-unto-men-weakness-that-they-may-be-humble` —["if men come unto me I will show unto them their weakness. I GIVE UNTO MEN WEAKNESS THAT THEY MAY BE HUMBLE"; God GIVES weakness — not merely permitted or accidental but given, on purpose, "that they may be humble"; our weaknesses are not flaws in the design but part of the design, the very means by which God keeps us humble enough to need Him; Moroni feared his clumsy writing would be mocked, and the Lord told him the clumsiness was the POINT — the weakness given to humble him]→ 12:27 (2 Cor 12:9; 1 Cor 1:27-31; Ex 4:10-12; Jacob 4:7)
- `doctrine:my-grace-is-sufficient-and-I-make-weak-things-become-strong` —["my grace is sufficient for all men that humble themselves before me; for if they humble themselves before me, and have faith in me, then will I MAKE WEAK THINGS BECOME STRONG unto them"; grace not partial or conditional on first becoming strong but SUFFICIENT, complete, for "all men that humble themselves" (Paul heard the same about his thorn, 2 Cor 12:9, "my strength is made perfect in weakness"); and the transformation real and active — not "I will overlook your weakness" but "I will MAKE the weak thing strong"; the weakness brought to Christ in humility and faith becomes the site of His strength; the whole gospel of the inadequate — your weakness is given to humble you, His grace sufficient when you humble yourself, the very weakness you bring He turns into strength; Moroni's "weak" words have moved millions]→ 12:26-27 (2 Cor 12:9-10; 1 Cor 1:27; Heb 11:34; Ether 12:37)
- `doctrine:faith-hope-and-charity-bring-unto-Christ-the-fountain-of-all-righteousness` —["faith, hope and charity bringeth unto me—the fountain of all righteousness"; the triad that leads to Christ (1 Cor 13:13, Moro 7); Moroni meditates on each — FAITH (the brother of Jared moved Mount Zerin, "if he had not had faith it would not have moved; wherefore thou workest AFTER men have faith" — God works after faith, the law restated), HOPE (the mansions of the Father, "man must hope, or he cannot receive an inheritance"), CHARITY (the love Christ had "even unto the laying down of thy life," "except men shall have charity they cannot inherit that place")]→ 12:28-34 (1 Cor 13:13; Moro 7:40-48; Matt 17:20; John 14:2)
- `doctrine:seeing-your-weakness-is-the-qualification-not-the-disqualification` —["because thou hast seen thy weakness thou shalt be made strong, even unto the sitting down in the place which I have prepared in the mansions of my Father"; seeing one's weakness is not the disqualification Moroni feared but the QUALIFICATION — the humility that grace requires; the very act of seeing his inadequacy is what opens the way to being made strong; the Lord's final word to Moroni ties the chapter together]→ 12:37 (Ether 12:27; 2 Cor 12:9-10; Mosiah 4:11; D&C 1:28)
- `doctrine:Moroni-saw-Jesus-face-to-face` —["ye shall know that I have seen Jesus, and that he hath talked with me face to face... even as a man telleth another in mine own language"; Moroni — like the brother of Jared, like Emer — saw Jesus, face to face, and spoke with Him as one man to another; the personal witness of the record's final author; he commends the reader to "seek this Jesus... that the grace of God the Father, and also the Lord Jesus Christ, and the Holy Ghost, which beareth record of them, may be and abide in you forever"; another witness for is-jesus-christ-god — Moroni's own face-to-face encounter]→ 12:38-41 (Gen 32:30; Ex 33:11; Num 12:8; Ether 3:13)

### from Ether 13
- `doctrine:the-New-Jerusalem-prophesied-at-the-moment-of-ruin-hope-set-against-destruction` —[at the very moment the Jaredite civilization slides into its final total war, Ether's recorded message is not about the destruction but about the GLORY that will rise on this same land — "a New Jerusalem... which should come down out of heaven, and the holy sanctuary of the Lord," "built up upon this land, unto the remnant of the seed of Joseph"; the hope set DELIBERATELY against the ruin; as one people destroys itself on this land, the prophet sees the consecrated city that will rise here in the latter days; the land's destiny is not the Jaredite catastrophe (one chapter) but the New Jerusalem; the darkest hour of the book contains its brightest prophecy — Ether saw it and recorded it so WE would know what the land is ultimately FOR]→ 13:2-8 (3 Ne 20:22; 3 Ne 21:23-24; D&C 84:2-5; Rev 21:1-2)
- `doctrine:the-type-of-Joseph-Gods-mercy-to-Josephs-seed-is-a-chain-from-Egypt-to-the-latter-day` —["as Joseph brought his father down into the land of Egypt, even so he died there; wherefore, the Lord brought a remnant of the seed of Joseph out of the land of Jerusalem, that he might be merciful unto the seed of Joseph that they should perish not, even as he was merciful unto the father of Joseph"; the mercy Joseph showed his father Jacob (bringing him to Egypt to preserve him) is a TYPE of God's mercy to Joseph's seed (bringing Lehi out of Jerusalem to preserve them); the pattern of preservation through the generations — Joseph saves his father, God saves Joseph's children, the remnant of Joseph will yet build the New Jerusalem; God's mercy a chain from Egypt to the latter day; "the first who shall be last, and last who shall be first" (13:12) — the despised remnant becomes the builder of the city that comes down from heaven]→ 13:6-12 (2 Ne 3:5-24; Gen 46:2-7; Mark 10:31; Jacob 5:63)
- `theme:the-prophet-in-the-cavity-of-a-rock-recording-the-destruction-he-cannot-prevent` —["they esteemed him as naught, and cast him out; and he hid himself in the cavity of a rock by day, and by night he went forth viewing the things which should come upon the people. And as he dwelt in the cavity of a rock he made the remainder of this record, viewing the destructions... by night"; the last prophet of a dying civilization, cast out, hiding in a rock, coming out under cover of darkness to WATCH the destruction and write it down; he cannot stop it but can witness it truthfully and preserve the record — exactly Mormon's "idle witness" posture (Morm 3:16); when the faithful can no longer save a people they can still bear witness for those who come after; one man hidden in a rock, the sole faithful witness of a civilization's self-destruction, writing in the dark; the prophet's final office is not to prevent the ruin he was unheard about but to make sure the truth of it survives — the whole book of Ether exists because a cast-out prophet hid in a rock and wrote by night]→ 13:13-14 (Morm 3:16; 1 Kgs 17:3; Mosiah 17:4; Jer 36:1-4)
- `doctrine:the-offer-of-salvation-extended-to-the-very-end-repent-and-the-whole-people-is-spared` —[even now, with the secret combinations risen and the land in total war, the Lord sends Ether with an offer: "if he would repent, and all his household, the Lord would give unto him his kingdom and spare the people"; the mercy extended to the very end — repent, and not only will you be spared but your WHOLE people will be spared; the destruction is never inevitable from God's side, always conditional on the refusal to repent; but Coriantumr "repented not" — the offer of salvation, for himself and everyone, was on the table, and he chose the war]→ 13:20, 22 (2 Ne 1:5-9; Hel 13:38; Ether 2:8-12; Matt 23:37)
- `doctrine:Coriantumrs-fate-to-outlive-everyone-and-die-a-stranger-among-the-people-who-replaced-you` —["otherwise they should be destroyed, and all his household save it were himself. And he should only live to see the fulfilling of the prophecies... another people receiving the land for their inheritance; and Coriantumr should receive a burial by them; and every soul should be destroyed save it were Coriantumr"; the prophecy of Coriantumr's fate — the lone survivor of a whole civilization, living only long enough to see the next people (the Mulekites/people of Zarahemla, Omni 1:21) inherit the land and to be buried among them; a fate worse than death — to outlive EVERYONE, watch your entire nation destroy itself, and die a stranger among the people who replaced you; the cost of refusing the offered mercy taken to its furthest extreme]→ 13:21 (Omni 1:21; Ether 14:24; Ether 15:29-32; Ether 11:21)

### from Ether 14
- `doctrine:the-curse-of-slippery-things-is-the-death-of-trust-and-community` —[the curse — tools and swords laid down couldn't be found "upon the morrow" (the slippery curse Samuel prophesied, Hel 13; that fell on the Nephites, Morm 1:18); and what it DOES to a society — "every man did cleave unto that which was his own, with his hands, and would not borrow neither would he lend; and every man kept the hilt of his sword in his right hand"; the curse on possessions is at root the DEATH OF TRUST — when nothing can be securely held, no one lends, no one shares, every man clutches his own with one hand and grips a sword with the other; the exact inversion of Zion (4 Ne 1:3, "all things common" because the love of God filled their hearts and trust was total); a people who abandon God lose the very capacity for community, because community runs on trust and trust has died; a society without God becomes a war of all against all in which even your possessions betray you]→ 14:1-2 (Hel 13:18-37; Morm 1:18; 4 Ne 1:3; Acts 4:32)
- `doctrine:the-secret-combination-devours-its-own-leaders-in-an-accelerating-cycle-of-murder` —[Gilead "received great strength to his army, because of secret combinations" — then "his high priest murdered him as he sat upon his throne," and a combination-assassin (Lib) murdered THAT man "in a secret pass" and took the kingdom; the combination promises power and delivers assassination; every man who rises by the oath of murder makes himself the next target; the throne gained by treachery held only until the next traitor is ready; organized evil cannot produce stable rule, only an accelerating cycle of murder, because the very thing it offers (power seized by killing) is available to everyone within it; the Jaredite leadership in its final phase a revolving door of assassins]→ 14:8-10 (Ether 9:1-12; Hel 6:38; Ether 8:15-18; Ether 9:26-27)
- `theme:war-becomes-an-environment-of-death-the-living-breathe-the-stench-of-their-own-dead` —["the whole face of the land was covered with the bodies of the dead. And so swift and speedy was the war that there was none left to bury the dead, but they did march forth from the shedding of blood to the shedding of blood, leaving the bodies of both men, women, and children strewed upon the face of the land, to become a prey to the worms of the flesh. And the scent thereof went forth upon the face of the land... wherefore the people became troubled by day and by night, because of the scent thereof"; the most visceral depiction of war's horror in the BoM — the dead too many to bury, the living marching "from the shedding of blood to the shedding of blood" without pause, the SMELL of the dead becoming the air the survivors breathe; war stopped being a series of battles and became the atmosphere — a people living inside the stench of their own dead; no romance, no glory, only a civilization rotting where it fell; Mormon abridges it without flinching, because the reader needs to see what the refusal to repent actually produces]→ 14:21-23 (Hosea 4:1-3; Isa 14:11; Morm 6:7-15; Ezek 35:8)
- `doctrine:the-fulness-of-his-wrath-is-the-self-prepared-destruction-God-removing-the-restraint` —["the Lord did visit them in the fulness of his wrath, and THEIR wickedness and abominations had PREPARED A WAY for their everlasting destruction"; two things hold together — this is "the fulness of his wrath" (the choice-land decree fulfilled, Ether 2:8-10), AND "their wickedness... had prepared a way"; the destruction is SELF-PREPARED — God's wrath not arbitrary intervention but the people given over to the consequences they built (the slippery curse, the combinations, the unrestrained war, the corpses — not God reaching down to smite but the natural fruit of a society that chose murder, secrecy, and the rejection of every prophet); "the fulness of his wrath" and "their wickedness prepared the way" are the same event from two sides; God's justice is precisely His allowing the self-consuming evil to run to its end (Morm 4:5); the wrath of God = the removal of the restraint that held the consequences back ("none to restrain them", 13:31)]→ 14:25 (Ether 2:8-10; Morm 4:5; Gal 6:7-8; Rom 1:24-28)
- `doctrine:the-vengeance-oath-is-the-engine-of-the-end` —["Shiz did not cease to pursue Coriantumr; for he had sworn to avenge himself upon Coriantumr of the blood of his brother"; the vengeance-oath drives the final phase; the same usurpation of God's prerogative ("vengeance is mine," Morm 3:15) that destroyed the Nephites now drives the Jaredites to their end; Shiz cannot stop because he has sworn to avenge, and the oath of vengeance once sworn becomes a chain that drags both the avenger and his enemy down to mutual destruction; the Jaredites destroyed not by a thunderbolt but by their own refusal to repent, their own combinations, and their own sworn vengeance]→ 14:24 (Morm 3:15; Rom 12:19; Ether 13:24; Deut 32:35)

### from Ether 15
- `doctrine:too-late-repentance-a-leaders-turning-cannot-save-a-people-who-will-not-repent` —[after two million lie dead Coriantumr "began to repent... and his soul mourned and refused to be comforted," and writes Shiz offering to GIVE UP THE KINGDOM "for the sake of the lives of the people" — exactly what the Lord asked in 13:20; but the offer that would have saved everyone THEN cannot save anyone NOW, because "the people repented not of their iniquity"; a leader's late turning cannot undo a nation's hardness; there is a point past which even genuine repentance cannot reverse consequences already set in motion, because they no longer depend on you alone; the window in which his repentance could have saved his nation had closed; and the vengeance-oath blocks even the peace he now offers (Shiz will accept only his death)]→ 15:1-6 (Ether 13:20-21; Mosiah 4:27; Alma 34:33-35; Hel 13:38)
- `doctrine:the-two-civilizations-end-at-the-same-hill-Ramah-is-Cumorah` —["the army of Coriantumr did pitch their tents by the hill Ramah; and it was that same hill where my father Mormon did hide up the records unto the Lord, which were sacred"; Ramah IS Cumorah — the two civilizations (Jaredites and Nephites, 1000+ years apart) make their final end AT THE SAME HILL; the law of the land made geographic; the hill where Moroni's father would hide the records and command the last Nephite ten thousand is where the last Jaredite armies gathered to annihilate each other; two peoples, the same covenant, the same ripening in iniquity, the same hill, the same end; Moroni abridging the Jaredite record stands in memory on the very ground where he watched his own people die; the repetition is the warning — this is what the land does twice to a people who fill it with wickedness]→ 15:11 (Morm 6:2; Omni 1:21; D&C 128:20; Ether 2:8-10)
- `theme:total-mobilization-the-whole-population-armed-for-mutual-annihilation` —["they were for the space of four years gathering together the people, that they might get all who were upon the face of the land... every one to the army which he would, with their wives and their children—both men, women and children being armed with weapons of war"; total mobilization carried to its absolute end — not soldiers but the ENTIRE population, every man, woman, and child, armed and arrayed for mutual annihilation; no civilians left, no remnant kept back; the whole people drawn into the machine of its own destruction]→ 15:12-15 (Morm 6:7-15; Ether 14:21-23; Ether 14:2)
- `theme:a-people-who-grieve-their-dead-every-night-and-cannot-stop-killing` —[they fight all day, retire at night, and "took up a howling and a lamentation for the loss of the slain of their people; and so great were their cries, their howlings and lamentations, that they did rend the air exceedingly"; night after night the air torn with mourning — and every morning they march back to kill and die again; the most terrible thing in the chapter — a people who GRIEVE their dead and yet CANNOT STOP killing; the grief is real, it does not turn them; "drunken with anger" — anger become an intoxication that overrides self-preservation, reason, and grief alike; a people drunk on anger cannot stop the war by reasoning about it]→ 15:16-22 (Moro 9:23; Prov 23:29-35; 2 Pet 2:19; Morm 6:7-15)
- `doctrine:the-Spirit-ceases-to-strive-and-the-people-are-given-up-the-end-state-of-the-rejected-prophet` —["the Spirit of the Lord had ceased striving with them, and Satan had full power over the hearts of the people; for they were given up unto the hardness of their hearts, and the blindness of their minds that they might be destroyed"; the end-state of a people who reject every prophet, embrace every combination, refuse every offered repentance — the Spirit CEASES to strive (Gen 6:3, the withdrawal before the Flood; Morm 5:16), they are "given up"/given over (Rom 1:24-28) to the hardness they chose, Satan having "full power over the hearts"; the most frightening doctrine in scripture, dramatized — so given up that Coriantumr's offered peace can't reach them, their own nightly grief can't turn them, the certainty of mutual destruction can't stop them; not God abandoning a people in cruelty but God finally honoring the choice they made over and over, withdrawing the Spirit they spent generations rejecting; the terror is the people no longer WANT to be saved]→ 15:19 (Gen 6:3; Morm 5:16; 2 Ne 26:11; Rom 1:24-28)
- `doctrine:drunken-with-anger-rage-as-an-intoxication-that-overrides-grief-and-self-preservation` —["they were drunken with anger, even as a man who is drunken with wine; and they slept again upon their swords"; anger become an intoxication — a drunk man cannot make himself sober by willing it, a people drunken with anger cannot stop the war by reasoning about it; the wrath has taken them over, overriding self-preservation, reason, and grief alike; the people fight on past all reason because rage has become an addiction]→ 15:22 (Moro 9:23; Prov 23:29-35; 2 Pet 2:19; Gal 5:19-21)
- `doctrine:Ethers-peace-the-faith-that-has-nothing-left-but-God-and-finds-it-enough` —["Whether the Lord will that I be translated, or that I suffer the will of the Lord in the flesh, it mattereth not, if it so be that I am saved in the kingdom of God. Amen"; set this serenity against everything that just happened — Ether has watched his ENTIRE civilization annihilate itself, every soul he ever knew, his whole world, and he alone is left; his last word is not despair, not rage, not even grief, but PEACE — it does not matter what becomes of me, translated or dead, only that I am saved in the kingdom of God; the faith that has nothing left but God and finds that God is enough; the raging people "drunken with anger" are all dead, the lone faithful witness who lost everything they had and more is at peace; a man can lose his entire world and remain serene if his treasure was never his world but his God; Ether's "it mattereth not" the opposite of the people's "given up" — they wanted only the kingdom and the vengeance, he wanted only the kingdom of God; the last word of the book is not the annihilation but a faithful man alone in the ruins saying nothing else matters at all]→ 15:32-34 (2 Tim 4:6-8; Phil 4:11-13; Hab 3:17-18; 3 Ne 28:7-9)

## — THE BOOK OF MORONI (the last book, Moroni's own) —

### from Moroni 1
- `doctrine:I-have-not-as-yet-perished-so-the-task-continues` —["I had supposed not to have written more, but I have not as yet perished... I write a few more things, contrary to that which I had supposed"; Moroni thought his work was done, the record finished — and then "I have not as yet perished," he is still alive; finding himself still living when he thought he'd be dead, he does not coast or wait passively but KEEPS WORKING; as long as you have "not as yet perished," there is more to give; survival treated not as a reprieve from labor but as an extension of it; the book of Moroni (incl. ch 7 on charity, ch 10 the promise) exists ONLY because Moroni, expecting death, lived a little longer and chose to fill the time with more writing rather than mere survival]→ 1:1, 4 (Morm 8:1-5; Moro 10:1-2; Ether 15:33-34; John 9:4)
- `doctrine:I-will-not-deny-the-Christ-faithfulness-over-safety` —["they put to death every Nephite that will not deny the Christ. And I, Moroni, will not deny the Christ; wherefore, I wander whithersoever I can for the safety of mine own life"; the simplest and starkest statement of fidelity in the BoM — deny Christ and live, confess Him and die; Moroni could buy his life with a single denial (the hunt would end, he could come out of hiding), all it would cost is the renunciation of the One he has seen face to face (Ether 12:39) — and he will not pay it; he wanders not to escape the demand to deny (already refused) but to stay alive long enough to finish the work; no drama, no boast of courage, just the plain fact — they kill those who won't deny, I won't deny, so I wander; faithfulness stripped to its bones — a steady daily refusal to save your life by a lie, even when the lie is the only thing between you and safety]→ 1:2-3 (Matt 10:32-33; 3 Ne 29:5; Mosiah 17:9-10; Rev 2:10)
- `doctrine:the-hunted-man-writes-for-the-good-of-his-hunters-descendants` —["I write a few more things... that perhaps they may be of worth unto my brethren, the Lamanites, in some future day, according to the will of the Lord"; the Lamanites are HUNTING HIM TO DEATH — and he writes for THEIR good, for the worth his words might have to their descendants "in some future day"; the same grace that closed Mormon's portion (Morm 7) — love of enemies to its furthest extreme; a man whose entire people were exterminated by the Lamanites, himself hunted by them, spends his last strength writing words to bless the Lamanites' posterity centuries later; he calls them "my brethren" — the people killing him; no bitterness, no curse, only the labor of love for a future generation of the very people who'd destroy him; the spirit of Christ Himself, who hunted to death prayed for those who killed Him]→ 1:4 (Morm 7:1-10; Matt 5:44; Luke 23:34; 2 Ne 3:11-12)

### from Moroni 2
- `doctrine:the-power-to-give-the-Holy-Ghost-is-real-and-delegated-but-exercised-in-Christs-name` —["ye shall have power that to him upon whom ye shall lay your hands, ye shall give the Holy Ghost; and in my name shall ye give it, for thus do mine apostles... on as many as they laid their hands, fell the Holy Ghost"; the power is REAL and DELEGATED — not metaphor, actual authority conferred on chosen men to bestow the Holy Ghost by the laying on of hands, confirmed to work; but the authority is NOT THEIR OWN — "in my name shall ye give it"; the power flows from Christ, the men conduits exercising His authority not generating it; "thus do mine apostles" grounds it in the universal pattern — what the Nephite Twelve do the Jerusalem apostles do, the order of the church one across the world]→ 2:1-3 (3 Ne 18:36-37; Acts 8:14-17; Acts 19:6; Matt 10:1)
- `doctrine:delegated-authority-is-drawn-down-by-mighty-prayer-not-switched-on-by-office` —["Ye shall call on the Father in my name, in mighty prayer; and AFTER YE HAVE DONE THIS ye shall have power"; the authority to act in God's name doesn't operate automatically or mechanically — preceded by "mighty prayer," the men calling on the Father before they exercise the gift; delegated power is real but drawn down by petition, not switched on by office; even the ordained must pray mightily to wield what Christ has given]→ 2:2 (Gen 4:26; Ether 4:15; 3 Ne 19:9-15; D&C 42:14)
- `doctrine:Moroni-preserves-the-ordinance-pattern-so-the-church-can-be-built-rightly` —[Moroni begins the short practical chapters (2-6) preserving exactly how Christ established His church — the ordinances and the order, recorded so the church could be built RIGHTLY; this first fills in what 3 Nephi referenced but didn't fully record (the words conferring the power to give the Holy Ghost); "the multitude heard it not, but the disciples heard it" marks the private commissioning of the leadership; the record built so the church can be rebuilt]→ 2:1-3 (3 Ne 11:21-22; 3 Ne 18:36-37; D&C 20:38-60; Eph 4:11-14)

### from Moroni 3
- `doctrine:the-form-of-ordination-is-plain-prayer-hands-the-name-of-Christ-and-the-Spirit` —["After they had prayed unto the Father in the name of Christ, they laid their hands upon them, and said: In the name of Jesus Christ I ordain you to be a priest... and they ordained them by the power of the Holy Ghost"; Moroni records the ordination in its bare, exact form, and the PLAINNESS is the point — no elaborate ceremony beyond the essentials (pray, lay on hands, speak the words, done by the Holy Ghost); building the record so the church can be reconstituted precisely, he preserves the irreducible core without ornament; the simplicity itself a testimony — the true church doesn't require elaborate machinery, it requires authority exercised in Christ's name by the power of the Holy Ghost; the form the restored Church would use (D&C 20:39, 60), preserved 14 centuries by a hunted man writing in hiding]→ 3:1-4 (D&C 20:38-60; D&C 18:32; Acts 6:6; Alma 6:1)
- `doctrine:the-office-is-a-charge-not-a-status-to-preach-repentance-and-remission-through-Christ` —[a priest or teacher is ordained "to preach repentance and remission of sins through Jesus Christ, by the endurance of faith on his name to the end"; the office is not an honor or status but a CHARGE, and the charge is the whole gospel in a sentence — turn people to Christ for forgiveness and enduring faith; every priest and teacher by the very words of his ordination pointed at the same single task; the ordination doesn't make a man important, it makes him an instrument of repentance and remission]→ 3:3 (3 Ne 27:20; Mosiah 18:20; Alma 5:62; D&C 4:5)
- `doctrine:ordination-is-done-by-the-power-of-the-Holy-Ghost-not-the-mans-own-authority` —["they ordained them by the power of the Holy Ghost, which was in them"; confirms what ch 2 established — the authority is real but not the men's own; they ordain not by their own dignity or office but by the power of the Holy Ghost; the whole act, from the opening prayer to the laying on of hands, the Spirit working through men who have first called on the Father; authority in Christ's church is plain, purposeful, powered by the Holy Ghost, not by the men who hold it]→ 3:4 (Moro 2:1-3; 1 Ne 13:37; Moro 6:9; D&C 20:60)

### from Moroni 4
- `doctrine:the-sacrament-prayer-preserved-exactly-the-ordinance-Christ-instituted` —["the manner of their elders and priests administering the flesh and blood of Christ... according to the commandments of Christ; wherefore we know the manner to be true"; Moroni preserves the sacrament prayer in its exact full form — the very words used in the Church today, unchanged 14 centuries because he wrote them while hiding for his life; the authority stated plainly — Christ Himself instituted it (3 Ne 18), the manner "true" because He gave it; not a human invention or evolving tradition but a commandment kept exactly]→ 4:1-3 (3 Ne 18:1-11; Luke 22:19; D&C 20:75-77)
- `doctrine:the-threefold-covenant-take-his-name-always-remember-him-keep-his-commandments` —[the partakers "witness unto thee... that they are willing to (1) take upon them the name of thy Son, and (2) always remember him, and (3) keep his commandments"; precisely the baptismal covenant (Mosiah 18:8-10) RENEWED; the sacrament is the weekly renewal of baptism — what was promised once at the water is re-witnessed each Sabbath at the table]→ 4:3 (Mosiah 18:8-10; 2 Ne 31:13; Mosiah 5:8; D&C 20:37)
- `doctrine:always-remember-him-that-they-may-always-have-his-Spirit` —["that they may eat in remembrance of the body of thy Son... and always remember him... that they may always have his Spirit to be with them"; the covenant is not one-directional — the partaker witnesses willingness, God answers with the abiding companionship of the Spirit; "always" appears twice and bears the weight — ALWAYS remember Him, that they may ALWAYS have His Spirit; the constancy of the remembering matched by the constancy of the promised presence; to always remember Christ is to always have His Spirit, the two bound; the whole purpose of the sacrament — a weekly act of remembrance renewing the baptismal covenant, securing the constant companionship of the Holy Ghost]→ 4:3 (3 Ne 18:7, 11; John 14:26; D&C 20:77; 2 Ne 32:5)
